		id:'',

  function ss_write(cnt, el, pos, width, height) {

      var str = '';

      if (!cnt.src) return;

      if (cnt.src.indexOf('.swf') != -1) {

          str = '<embed width="' + width + '" height="' + height + '" flashvars="url=' + cnt.url + '" wmode="opaque" quality="high" src="' + cnt.src + '" type="application/x-shockwave-flash">';

      } else {

          str = '<a target="_blank" id="'+cnt.id+'" href="' + cnt.url + '"><img width="' + width + '" height="' + height + '" border="0" src="' + cnt.src + '"></a>';

      }

      el.html(str).show();

      if (ss_source[pos].script) {

          document.write('<script type="text/javascript" src="' + ss_source[pos].script + '"></sc'+'ript>');

      } else if (cnt.script && cnt.script != '') {

          document.write('<script type="text/javascript" src="' + cnt.script + '"></scr'+'ipt>');

      }

  };

  var ssAlternate = new GGrandomAlternate("source_ss", ss_source);

  ssAlternate.callback = function(pos) {

      window.currentPos = pos;

    ss_write(ss_source[pos].cnt1, $('.ad17173FullVerCorner:eq(0)'), pos, 1000, 120);

      ss_write(ss_source[pos].cnt2, $('.ad17173FullVerCorner:eq(1)'), pos, 240, 400);

  };

  ssAlternate.execute();

})();</script>
